2024-08-11 01:48:24.987 +03:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (1ms) [Parameters=[@__p_0='?' (DbType = Int32)], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT t."Id", t."CategoryId", t."Description", t."Dimensions", t."Keywords", t."LightSource", t."Material", t."Name", t."PercentOff", t."Price", t."StripeId", t."Visible", v."Id", v."ColorCode", v."Name", v."ProductId"
FROM (
    SELECT p."Id", p."CategoryId", p."Description", p."Dimensions", p."Keywords", p."LightSource", p."Material", p."Name", p."PercentOff", p."Price", p."StripeId", p."Visible", gen_random_uuid() AS c
    FROM "Product" AS p
    ORDER BY gen_random_uuid()
    LIMIT @__p_0
) AS t
LEFT JOIN "Variant" AS v ON t."Id" = v."ProductId"
WHERE t."CategoryId" <> 4
ORDER BY t.c, t."Id"
